222a6(ka): / gsed bris can dang / 'bre ru rtsa yag glung yad grong chang gi lag bris yig nag dos rnying / bha daum ma gtegs ga dum med pa'i sad gcig dang // bal gyung dgen pa'i bka' 'gyud gras su yed pa'i lag bhris yig nag 'phrul / 
222b1(ka): / pad can dang bcas la 'dra bsdud byas te/ bris pa'i chad lhag dang / mngon gsal can gyi rkyen ma then degs cha brkangs byas yod kyang / gzhan pa rnams ma des stag chen can la/ seMr bzhag las bces brgyud byas me// su / 
222b2(ka): la'i bka' 'gyur brgyud dam nang nad gnyan 'thing gi gted lugs su bzhag pa bzhin/ rgi bzhi mdzod lnga'i dse rnying phyegs bsgrigs/ kyi pad grangs bapad zhus bsgrigs byas yod kyang ddung ma rtegs dbang gis chad / 
222b3(ka): lhag segs yod nges te/ spyi la rbyad sngon lo nga lnga brgya ldag nas gangs can bad kyi yrul du yo go' par cang 'jugs bsgun dang // se gzhi legs bgrigs byas pa'i 'grems pe la yongs khyab byed srel dad zien na'ang // 
222b4(ka): g.sung dung boan gyi ds gzhi' bsdu bsgrigs byed pa'o ga rskabs kyi ched yug de tshal byung med pas/ 'did phyegs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la mig nyes len gzhi dken pas gam kha gsad du yin pa dang / rges su de / 
222b5(ka): zhus bsgrigs pa tche yang mkhyen dbyed dab 'byams pa min chad/ 'di'i thad mthun rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb tu dal brling 'grig pa dang ma byung na/ phyegs gang so'i chad yug dang gnas sangs tsha las brgal ba'i /
